 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;3. Summary of Significant Accounting Policies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Basis of Presentation and Consolidation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27.35pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The accompanying consolidated&#13;financial statements for Eastside Distilling, Inc. and subsidiaries were prepared in accordance with accounting principles generally&#13;accepted in the United States of America (GAAP). The consolidated financial statements include the accounts of Eastside Distilling,&#13;Inc.&amp;#8217;s wholly-owned subsidiaries, including, MotherLode LLC, Big Bottom Distilling, LLC, Outlandish Beverages LLC, LLC, Redneck&#13;Riviera Whiskey Co., LLC, and Craft Canning + Bottling, LLC (beginning as of January 11, 2019) and the Azu&amp;#241;ia tequila assets&#13;(beginning September 12, 2019). All intercompany balances and transactions have been eliminated in consolidation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Segment Reporting&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company determined&#13;its operating segment on the same basis that it uses to evaluate its performance internally. The Company has one business activity,&#13;packaging, producing, marketing and distributing alcoholic beverages and operates as one segment. The Company&amp;#8217;s chief operating&#13;decision makers, its chief executive officer and chief financial officer, review the Company&amp;#8217;s operating results on an aggregate&#13;basis for purposes of allocating resources and evaluating financial performance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Use of Estimates&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The preparation of financial&#13;statements in accordance with GAAP requires management to make estimates and assumptions that affect the reported amounts of assets&#13;and liabilities and disclosure of contingent assets and liabilities at the date of the financial statements and the reported amounts&#13;of revenues and expenses during the reporting period. Actual results could differ from those estimates.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenue Recognition&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Net sales include product&#13;sales, less excise taxes and customer programs and incentives. The Company recognizes revenue by applying the following steps in&#13;accordance with Accounting Standards Codification (&amp;#8220;ASC&amp;#8221;) Topic 606 &amp;#8211; &lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&lt;/i&gt;:&#13;(1) identify the contract with a customer; (2) identify the performance obligations in the contract; (3) determine the transaction&#13;price; (4) allocate the transaction price to each performance obligation in the contract; and (5) recognize revenue when each performance&#13;obligation is satisfied.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company recognizes&#13;sales when merchandise is shipped from a warehouse directly to wholesale customers (except in the case of a consignment sale).&#13;For consignment sales, which include sales to the Oregon Liquor Control Commission (OLCC), the Company recognizes sales upon the&#13;consignee&amp;#8217;s shipment to the customer. Postage and handling charges billed to customers are also recognized as sales upon&#13;shipment of the related merchandise. Shipping terms are generally FOB shipping point, and title passes to the customer at the time&#13;and place of shipment or purchase by customers at a retail location. For consignment sales, title passes to the consignee concurrent&#13;with the consignee&amp;#8217;s shipment to the customer. The customer has no cancellation privileges after shipment or upon purchase&#13;at retail locations, other than customary rights of return. The Company excludes sales tax collected and remitted to various states&#13;from sales and cost of sales.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Customer Programs &lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Customer programs, which&#13;include customer promotional discount programs, customer incentives, and broker commissions, are a common practice in the alcoholic&#13;beverage industry. The Company makes these payments to customers and incurs these costs to promote sales of products and to maintain&#13;competitive pricing. Amounts paid in connection with customer programs and incentives are recorded as reductions to net sales or&#13;as sales and marketing expenses in accordance with ASC 606 - &lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers,&lt;/i&gt; based on the nature&#13;of the expenditure. Amounts paid to customers totaled $1.0 million and $0.6 million for the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019,&#13;respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Excise Taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company is responsible&#13;for compliance with the Alcohol and Tobacco Tax and Trade Bureau (&amp;#8220;TTB&amp;#8221;) regulations, which includes making timely&#13;and accurate excise tax payments. The Company is subject to periodic compliance audits by the TTB. Individual states also impose&#13;excise taxes on alcoholic beverages in varying amounts. The Company calculates its excise tax expense based upon units produced&#13;and on its understanding of the applicable excise tax laws. Excise taxes totaled $0.1 million and $0 million for the years ended&#13;December 31, 2020 and 2019, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cost of Sales&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Cost of sales consists&#13;of the costs of ingredients utilized in the production of spirits, manufacturing labor and overhead, warehousing rent, packaging,&#13;and in-bound freight charges. Ingredients account for the largest portion of the cost of sales, followed by packaging and production&#13;costs.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Sales and Marketing Expenses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The following expenses&#13;are included in sales and marketing expenses in the accompanying consolidated statements of operations: media advertising costs,&#13;promotional costs of value-added packaging, salary and benefit expenses, travel and entertainment expenses for the sales, brand&#13;and sales support workforce and promotional activity expenses.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;General and Administrative Expenses&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The following expenses&#13;are included in general and administrative expenses in the accompanying condensed consolidated statements of operations: salary&#13;and benefit expenses, travel and entertainment expenses for executive and administrative staff, rent and utilities, professional&#13;fees, insurance, and amortization and depreciation expense. General and administrative costs are expensed as incurred.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-Based Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company recognizes&#13;as compensation expense all stock-based awards issued to employees. The compensation cost is measured based on the grant-date fair&#13;value of the related stock-based awards and is recognized over the service period of stock-based awards, which is generally the&#13;same as the vesting period. The fair value of stock options is determined using the Black-Scholes valuation model, which estimates&#13;the fair value of each award on the date of grant based on a variety of assumptions including expected stock price volatility,&#13;expected terms of the awards, risk-free interest rate, and dividend rates, if applicable. Stock-based awards issued to nonemployees&#13;are recorded at fair value on the measurement date and are subject to periodic market adjustments at the end of each reporting&#13;period and as the underlying stock-based awards vest. Stock-based compensation was $0.3 million and $0.7 million for the years&#13;ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Discontinued Operations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company reports discontinued&#13;operations by applying the following criteria in accordance with ASC Topic 205-20 &amp;#8211; &lt;i&gt;Presentation of Financial Statements&#13;&amp;#8211; Discontinued Operations&lt;/i&gt;: (1) Component of an entity; (2) Held for sale criteria; and (3) Strategic shift.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On December 31, 2019, management&#13;made a strategic shift to focus the Company&amp;#8217;s sales and marketing efforts on the nationally branded product platform, resulting&#13;in the decision to close all four of its retail stores in the Portland, Oregon area. Although this decision meets the criteria&#13;(1) and (3) for reporting discontinued operations, it did not meet the (2) Held for sale criteria until the retail stores were&#13;closed or abandoned, which occurred by March 31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On October 29, 2020, the&#13;Company announced its intent to divest its Redneck Riviera Spirits business. The Company signed a non-binding term sheet between&#13;Eastside and Rich Marks, LLC, Redneck Riviera Whiskey Co, LLC (&amp;#8220;RRWC&amp;#8221;), John D. Rich Tisa Trust and Redneck Spirits&#13;Group, LLC (collectively the buyers referred to as &amp;#8220;RSG&amp;#8221;) whereby RSG would pay a termination fee as well as purchase&#13;certain assets from the Company which could include raw materials and finished goods. The total consideration was estimated to&#13;be $8.1 million inclusive of a $3 million dollar termination fee and the remainder of proceeds from selling RSG raw materials and&#13;finished goods. The divesture is subject to negotiation and execution of definitive agreements. On February 8, 2021, the Company&#13;completed the sale of its Redneck Riviera Spirits business.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As of and for the year&#13;ended December 31, 2020, the assets, liabilities, revenue, expenses and cash flows from retail operations and the RRWC business&#13;have been classified as discontinued operations separately from continuing operations. For comparative purposes, prior period amounts&#13;have been reclassified to conform to current period presentation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Income and expense related&#13;to discontinued retail operations and the Redneck Riviera Spirits business were as follows for the years ended December 31, 2020&#13;and 2019:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;60&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-left: 20pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Total current liabilities&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;18&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;715&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Lease liability - less current portion&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;71&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;113&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; padding-left: 20pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Total Liabilities&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;89&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;828&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and Cash Equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Cash equivalents are considered&#13;to be highly liquid investments with maturities of three months or less at the time of the purchase. The Company had no cash equivalents&#13;as of December 31, 2020 and 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Financial instruments that&#13;potentially subject the Company to concentrations of credit risk consist principally of trade receivables. As of December 31, 2020,&#13;one distributor represented 14% of trade receivables. As of December 31, 2019, two distributors represented 40% of trade receivables.&#13;Sales to one distributor accounted for 18% of consolidated sales for the year ended December 31, 2020. Sales to one distributor&#13;accounted for 16% of consolidated sales for the year ended December 31, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair Value Measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;GAAP defines fair value,&#13;establishes a framework for measuring fair value, and requires certain disclosures about fair value measurements. GAAP permits&#13;an entity to choose to measure many financial instruments and certain other items at fair value and contains financial statement&#13;presentation and disclosure requirements for assets and liabilities for which the fair value option is elected. As of December&#13;31, 2020 and 2019, management has not elected to report any of the Company&amp;#8217;s assets or liabilities at fair value under the&#13;&amp;#8220;fair value option&amp;#8221; provided by GAAP.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The hierarchy of fair value&#13;valuation techniques under GAAP provides for three levels: Level 1 provides the most reliable measure of fair value, whereas Level&#13;3, if applicable, generally would require significant management judgment. The three levels for categorizing assets and liabilities&#13;under GAAP&amp;#8217;s fair value measurement requirements are as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 62px&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 62px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 1:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using cash or unadjusted quoted prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 2:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using inputs other than quoted prices that are observable for the applicable asset or liability, either directly or indirectly, such as quoted prices for similar (as opposed to identical) assets or liabilities in active markets and quoted prices for identical or similar assets or liabilities in markets that are not active.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 3:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using unobservable inputs that are significant to the fair value measurement and reflect management&amp;#8217;s own assumptions regarding the applicable asset or liability.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;None of the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;assets or liabilities were measured at fair value as of December 31, 2020 or 2019. However, GAAP requires the disclosure of fair&#13;value information about financial instruments that are not measured at fair value. Financial instruments consist principally of&#13;trade receivables, accounts payable, accrued liabilities, notes payable, convertible note payable and the secured credit facility.&#13;The estimated fair value of trade receivables, accounts payable, and accrued liabilities approximates their carrying value due&#13;to the short period of time to their maturities. As of December 31, 2020 and 2019, the Company&amp;#8217;s notes are payable at fixed&#13;rates and their carrying value approximates fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Items Measured at Fair Value on a Nonrecurring&#13;Basis&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Certain assets and liabilities&#13;acquired in a business acquisition are valued at fair value at the date of acquisition.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Inventories&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Inventories primarily consist&#13;of bulk and bottled liquor and merchandise and are stated at the lower of cost or market. Cost is determined using an average costing&#13;methodology, which approximates cost under the first-in, first-out (FIFO) method. A portion of inventory is held by certain independent&#13;distributors on consignment until it is sold to a third party. The Company regularly monitors inventory quantities on hand and&#13;records write-downs for excess and obsolete inventories based primarily on the Company&amp;#8217;s estimated forecast of product demand&#13;and production requirements. Such write-downs establish a new cost basis of accounting for the related inventory.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Property and Equipment&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Property and equipment&#13;is stated at cost less accumulated depreciation and amortization. Depreciation is computed using the straight-line method over&#13;the estimated useful lives of the assets, ranging from three to seven years. Amortization of leasehold improvements is computed&#13;using the straight-line method over the life of the lease or the useful lives of the assets, whichever is shorter. The cost and&#13;related accumulated depreciation and amortization of property and equipment sold or otherwise disposed of are removed from the&#13;accounts and any gain or loss is reported as current period income or expense. The costs of repairs and maintenance are expensed&#13;as incurred.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Intangible Assets / Goodwill&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company accounts for&#13;certain intangible assets at cost. Management reviews these intangible assets for probable impairment whenever events or circumstances&#13;indicate that the carrying amount of such assets may not be recoverable. If there is an indication of impairment, management would&#13;prepare an estimate of future cash flows (undiscounted and without interest charges) expected to result from the use of the asset&#13;and its eventual disposition. If these estimated cash flows were less than the carrying amount, an impairment loss would be recognized&#13;to write down the asset to its estimated fair value. The Company performed a qualitative assessment of certain of its intangible&#13;assets as of December 31, 2020 and determined that they were not impaired.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Long-lived Assets&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company accounts for&#13;long-lived assets, including certain intangible assets, at amortized cost. Management reviews long-lived assets for probable impairment&#13;whenever events or circumstances indicate that the carrying amount of such assets may not be recoverable. If there is an indication&#13;of impairment, management would prepare an estimate of future cash flows (undiscounted and without interest charges) expected to&#13;result from the use of the asset and its eventual disposition. If these estimated cash flows were less than the carrying amount&#13;of the asset, an impairment loss would be recognized to write down the asset to its estimated fair value. The Company performed&#13;a qualitative assessment of certain of its intangible assets as of December 31, 2020 and determined that they were not impaired.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income Taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The provision for income&#13;taxes is based on income and expenses as reported for financial statement purposes using the &amp;#8220;asset and liability method&amp;#8221;&#13;for accounting for deferred taxes. Deferred tax assets and liabilities are recognized for the future tax consequences attributable&#13;to differences between the financial statement carrying amounts of existing assets and liabilities and their respective tax bases.&#13;Deferred tax assets and liabilities are reflected at currently enacted income tax rates applicable to the period in which the deferred&#13;tax assets or liabilities are expected to be realized or settled.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As changes in tax laws&#13;or rates are enacted, deferred tax assets and liabilities are adjusted through the provision for income taxes. A valuation allowance,&#13;if needed, reduces deferred tax assets to the amount expected to be realized. As of December 31, 2020 and 2019, the Company established&#13;valuation allowances against its net deferred tax assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27.35pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Income tax positions that&#13;meet the &amp;#8220;more-likely-than-not&amp;#8221; recognition threshold are measured at the largest amount of income tax benefit that&#13;is more than 50% likely to be realized upon settlement with the applicable taxing authority. The portion of the benefits associated&#13;with income tax positions taken that exceeds the amount measured as described above would be reflected as a liability for unrecognized&#13;income tax benefits in the accompanying consolidated balance sheets along with any associated interest and penalties that would&#13;be payable to the taxing authorities upon examination. Interest and penalties associated with unrecognized income tax benefits&#13;would be classified as additional income taxes in the accompanying consolidated statements of operations. There were no unrecognized&#13;income tax benefits, nor any interest and penalties associated with unrecognized income tax benefits, accrued or expensed at and&#13;for the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company files federal&#13;income tax returns in the United States. and various state income tax returns. The Company is no longer subject to examinations&#13;by the related tax authorities for the Company&amp;#8217;s U.S. federal and state income tax returns for years prior to 2013.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Comprehensive Income&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company does not have&#13;any reconciling other comprehensive income items for the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Accounts Receivable Factoring Program&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company has entered into&#13;two accounts receivable factoring programs. One for its spirits customers (the &amp;#8220;spirits program&amp;#8221;) and another for its&#13;co-packing customers (the &amp;#8220;co-packing program&amp;#8221;). Under the programs, the Company has the option to sell certain customer&#13;account receivables in advance of payment for 75% (spirits program) or 85% (co-packing program) of the amount due. When the customer&#13;remits payment, the Company receives the remaining balance. For the spirits program, interest is charged on the advanced 75% payment&#13;at a rate of 2.4% for the first 30 days plus 1.44% for each additional ten-day period. For the co-packing program, interest is&#13;charged against the greater of $0.5 million or the total funds advanced at a rate of 5% plus the prime rate published in the Wall&#13;Street Journal. Under the terms of both agreements, the factoring provider has full recourse against the Company should the customer&#13;fail to pay the invoice. In accordance with ASC Topic 860 &amp;#8211; &lt;i&gt;Transfers and Servicing&lt;/i&gt;, the Company has concluded that&#13;these agreements have met all three conditions identified in ASC Topic 860-10-40-5 (a) &amp;#8211; (c) and have accounted for this&#13;activity as a sale. Given the quality of the factored accounts, the Company has not recognized a recourse obligation. In certain&#13;limited instances, the Company may provide collection services on the factored accounts but does not receive any fees for acting as&#13;the collection agent, and as such, the Company has not recognized a service obligation asset or liability. The Company factored $7.9&#13;million of invoices and incurred $0.2 million in fees associated with the factoring programs during the year ended December 31,&#13;2020. As of December 31, 2020, the Company had $0.2 million factored invoices outstanding.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27.35pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Recently Adopted Accounting Pronouncements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;4. Business Acquisitions&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;During the fiscal year 2019, the&#13;Company completed the following acquisitions:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;u&gt;Craft Canning + Bottling&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On January 11, 2019, the Company&#13;completed the acquisition of Craft Canning &amp;#38; Bottling, LLC (&amp;#8220;Craft Canning&amp;#8221;), a Portland, Oregon-based provider of bottling&#13;and canning services. The Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated financial statements for the year ended December 31, 2019 include Craft Canning&amp;#8217;s&#13;results of operations from the acquisition date of January 11, 2019 through December 31, 2019. The Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated financial&#13;statements reflect the final purchase accounting adjustments in accordance with ASC Topic 805 - &lt;i&gt;Business Combinations&lt;/i&gt;, whereby&#13;the purchase price was allocated to the assets acquired and liabilities assumed based upon their estimated fair values on the acquisition&#13;date.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;4,845&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Intangible assets are recorded&#13;at estimated fair value, as determined by management based on available information. The fair value assigned to the customer list intangible&#13;asset was determined through the use of the income approach, specifically the relief from royalty and the multi-period excess earning&#13;methods. The major assumptions used in arriving at the estimated identifiable intangible asset value included management&amp;#8217;s estimates&#13;of future cash flows, discounted at an appropriate rate of return which is based on the weighted average cost of capital for both the&#13;Company and other market participants, projected customer attrition rates, as well as applicable royalty rates for comparable assets.&#13;The useful lives for intangible assets were determined based upon the remaining useful economic lives of the tangible assets that are&#13;expected to contribute directly or indirectly to future cash flows. The customer relationships estimated useful life is seven years.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company incurred Craft Canning-related&#13;acquisition costs of $0.1 million during the year ended December 31, 2019 that have been recorded in general and administrative expenses&#13;in the consolidated statements of operations. The results of the Craft Canning acquisition are included in the consolidated financial&#13;statements from the date of acquisition through December 31, 2019. The revenue and net income (including transaction costs) of Craft Canning&#13;operations included in the consolidated statements of operations were $7.1 million and $0.4 million, respectively, for the period from&#13;January 11, 2019 through December 31, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;u&gt;Azu&amp;#241;ia Tequila&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On September 12, 2019, the Company&#13;completed the acquisition of the Azu&amp;#241;ia brand, the direct sales team, existing product inventory, supply chain relationships and&#13;contractual agreements from Intersect Beverage, LLC (&amp;#8220;Intersect&amp;#8221;), an importer and distributor of tequila and related products.&#13;The Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated financial statements as of and for the year ended December 31, 2019 include the Azu&amp;#241;ia assets and&#13;results of operations. For the year ended December 31, 2019, the Azu&amp;#241;ia results of operations are included from the acquisition date&#13;of September 12, 2019 through December 31, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The acquisition was structured&#13;as an all-stock transaction, provided that the Company may, at its election, pay a portion of the consideration in cash or by executing&#13;a three-year promissory note if the issuance of stock would require the Company to hold a vote of its stockholders under the applicable&#13;Nasdaq rules. Subject to compliance with applicable Nasdaq rules, the initial consideration, will be payable approximately 18 months following&#13;the closing and will consist of 850,000 shares of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock at a stipulated value of $6.00 per share, 350,000 shares&#13;of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock based on the Company&amp;#8217;s stock price twelve months after the close of the transaction, and additional&#13;shares based on the Azu&amp;#241;ia business achieving certain revenue targets and the Company&amp;#8217;s stock price 18 months after the close&#13;of the transaction. The Company has also agreed to issue additional stock consideration (subject to compliance with applicable Nasdaq&#13;rules) of up to $1.5 million upon the Azu&amp;#241;ia business achieving revenue of at least $9.45 million in the period commencing on the&#13;13th month following the closing and ending on the 24th month following the closing.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company&amp;#8217;s consolidated&#13;financial statements reflect the final purchase accounting adjustments in accordance with ASC Topic 805, whereby the purchase price was&#13;allocated to the assets acquired based upon their estimated fair values on the acquisition date. The Company estimated the purchase price&#13;based on weighted probabilities of future results and recorded deferred consideration payable of $12.8 million on the acquisition date&#13;that will be remeasured to fair value at each reporting date until the contingencies are resolved, with the changes in fair value recognized&#13;in earnings. The Company remeasured the deferred consideration payable for the period ended December 31, 2019 and increased the liability&#13;by $2.7 million to a balance of $15.5 million. No adjustment was made to the deferred consideration payable for the period ended December&#13;31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

   &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt; padding-left: 10pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Intangible assets - brand&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;11,945&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Total&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;12,781&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Intangible assets are recorded&#13;at estimated fair value, as determined by management based on available information. The fair value assigned to the brand intangible asset&#13;was determined through the use of the market approach. The major assumptions used in arriving at the estimated identifiable intangible&#13;asset value included category averages for comparable acquisitions, including multiples of annual sales and dollars per case sold. The&#13;brand has an indefinite life and will not be amortized.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company incurred Azu&amp;#241;ia-related&#13;acquisition costs of $0.2 million during the year ended December 31, 2019 that have been recorded in general and administrative expenses&#13;in the consolidated statements of operations. The results of the Azu&amp;#241;ia asset acquisition are included in the consolidated financial&#13;statements from the date of acquisition through December 31, 2019. The sales of Azu&amp;#241;ia products included in the consolidated statements&#13;of operations were $1.1 million for the period from September 12, 2019 through December 31, 2019. Sales were $2.9 million for the year&#13;ended December 31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;During 2020, it was determined&#13;that certain costs related to branding services previously capitalized had no further value and were written off. The net value&#13;of these services at the time of the write down was $0.4 million. The remaining deposits of $0.1 million represent office and retail&#13;space lease deposits. In September 2020, the Company had received the remaining balance of the notes receivable from Wineonline.com.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;9. Leases&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company has various&#13;lease agreements in place for facilities and equipment. Terms of these leases include, in some instances, scheduled rent increases,&#13;renewals, purchase options and maintenance costs, and vary by lease. These lease obligations expire at various dates through 2025.&#13;The Company determines if an arrangement is a lease at inception. The Company does not currently have any finance leases. As the&#13;rate implicit in each lease is not readily determinable, the Company uses its incremental borrowing rate based on information available&#13;at commencement to determine the present value of the lease payments. Right-of-use assets and lease liabilities are recognized&#13;at commencement date based on the present value of lease payments over the lease term. Leases with an initial term of 12 months&#13;or less (&amp;#8220;short-term leases&amp;#8221;) are not recorded on the balance sheet and are recognized on a straight-line basis over&#13;the lease term. In September 2020, the Company entered into two new lease agreements for canning and bottling production facilities&#13;in Seattle and Denver. Both leases contain fixed payments that increase over the term of their respective agreement. As of December&#13;31, 2020, the amount of right-of-use assets and lease liabilities were $1.3 million and $1.3 million, respectively. Aggregate lease&#13;expense for the year ended December 31, 2020 was $0.8 million, consisting of $0.5 million in operating lease expense for lease&#13;liabilities and $0.3 million in short-term lease cost.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

Interest is paid monthly.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 16%; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;2,300&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 16%; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;2,300&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 1%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Notes payable bearing interest at 1.00%. The notes&amp;#8217; principal, plus any accrued and unpaid interest is due May 1, 2022. Loan payments are deferred six months from start of loan. To help ensure adequate liquidity in light of uncertainties posed by the COVID-19 pandemic, the Company received this loan under the Small Business Administration&amp;#8217;s (&amp;#8220;SBA&amp;#8221;) Paycheck Protection Program (&amp;#8220;PPP&amp;#8221;).&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;1,052&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Notes payable bearing interest at 1.00%. The notes&amp;#8217; principal, plus any accrued and unpaid interest is due May 1, 2022. Loan payments are deferred six months from start of loan. The Company received this loan under the SBA&amp;#8217;s PPP.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;396&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Convertible note payable bearing interest at 9.00%. The note principal, plus any accrued and unpaid interest is due December 31, 2020. The note has a voluntary conversion feature where in the event of an equity offering of at least $1.0 million at a purchase price of at least $4.25 (subject to adjustment), the noteholder shall have the right to participate in the financing by converting all outstanding principal and accrued and unpaid interest on this note into the securities to be sold in the offering.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;254&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Notes payable bearing interest at 5.00%. Principal and accrued interest is payable in six equal installments on each six-month anniversary of the issuance date of January 11, 2019. The notes are secured by the security interests and subordinated to the Company&amp;#8217;s senior indebtedness.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;370&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;650&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable bearing interest of 5.2%. The note has a 46-month term with maturity in May 2023. Principal and accrued interest are paid in accordance with a monthly amortization schedule. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;129&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;177&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable bearing interest of 4.45%. The note has a 34-month term with maturity in May 2022. Principal and accrued interest are paid in accordance with a monthly amortization schedule. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning and includes debt covenants requiring a Current Ratio of 1.75 to 1.00 and a Debt Service Coverage Ratio of 1.25 to 1.00. Craft Canning must also provide annual financial statements and tax returns. Craft Canning was in compliance with all debt covenants as of December 31, 2020.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;163&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;266&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable under a revolving line of credit bearing variable interest starting at 5.5%. The note has a 12-month term with principal and accrued interest due in lump sum in July 2020. The borrowing limit is $0.3 million. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;50&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable under a revolving line of credit bearing variable interest starting at 3.25%. The note has a 15-month term with principal and accrued interest due in lump sum in January 2022. The borrowing limit is $0.5 million. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;500&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable bearing interest of 4.14%. The note has a 60-month term with maturity in July 2024. Principal and accrued interest are paid in accordance with a monthly amortization schedule. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;146&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;183&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable bearing interest of 3.91%. The note has a 60-month term with maturity in August 2024. Principal and accrued interest are paid in accordance with a monthly amortization schedule. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;226&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;282&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory note payable bearing interest of 3.96%. The note has a 60-month term with maturity in November 2024. Principal and accrued interest are paid in accordance with a monthly amortization schedule. The note is secured by the assets of Craft Canning.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;241&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;295&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Secured line of credit promissory note for a revolving line of credit in the aggregate principal amount of $2.0 million. The Note matures on April 15, 2020 and may be prepaid in whole or in part at any time without penalty or premium. Repayment of the Note is subject to acceleration in the event of an event of default. The Company may use the proceeds to purchase tequila for its Azu&amp;#241;ia product line and for general corporate purposes, as approved by the Holder. The obligations of the Company under the Note are secured by certain inventory of the Company and its subsidiaries and the Company&amp;#8217;s membership interests in Craft Canning. In addition, the Note is guaranteed by the Company&amp;#8217;s subsidiaries Craft Canning and Big Bottom Distilling. The Note and the accompanying guaranty restrict Craft Canning from incurring any new indebtedness, other than trade debt incurred in the ordinary course of business, until the Note is repaid in full. The obligations under the Note are subordinate and junior in right and priority of payment to the Company&amp;#8217;s obligations under the Company&amp;#8217;s Credit and Security Agreement with the KFK Children&amp;#8217;s Trust dated May 10, 2018. The Note was paid in full in January 2020.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;946&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Promissory notes payable bearing interest between 2.99% - 3.14%. The notes have 60-month terms with maturity dates between February 2019 &amp;#8211; June 2020. Principal and accrued interest are paid monthly. The notes are secured by the specific vehicle underlying the loan.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Total notes payable&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;5,523&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;5,413&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: white&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Less current portion&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;(3,830&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 1.5pt solid; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;(1,819&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 1.5pt&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;)&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;  &lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom; background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Long-term portion of notes payable&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;3,594&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;  Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company paid $0.1 million&#13;and $0.2 million in interest on its notes payable during the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, respectively.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Maturities on notes payable as&#13;of December 31, 2020 were as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
