&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;11. Secured Credit Facility&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On January 15, 2020, the&#13;Company entered into a loan agreement (the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Loan Agreement&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;) between the Company which includes its wholly-owned&#13;subsidiaries MotherLode LLC, an Oregon limited liability company, Big Bottom Distilling, LLC, an Oregon limited liability company,&#13;Craft Canning + Bottling, LLC, an Oregon limited liability company, Redneck Riviera Whiskey Co., LLC, a Tennessee limited liability&#13;company, and Outlandish Beverages LLC, an Oregon limited liability company collectively, (the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Borrowers&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221; and&#13;each a &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Borrower&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;) and Live Oak Banking Company (&amp;#8220;Live Oak&amp;#8221;), a North Carolina banking corporation&#13;(the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Lender&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;) to refinance existing debt of the Borrowers and to provide funding for general working capital&#13;purposes. Under the Loan Agreement, the Lender has committed to make up to two loan advances to the Borrowers in an aggregate&#13;principal amount not to exceed the lesser of (i) $8.0 million and (ii) a borrowing base equal to 85% of the appraised value of the&#13;Borrowers&amp;#8217; eligible inventory of whisky in barrels or totes less an amount equal to all service fees or rental payments owed&#13;by the Borrowers during the 90 day period immediately succeeding the date of determination to any warehouses or bailees holding&#13;eligible inventory (the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Loan&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Loan matures on January&#13;14, 2021 and all amounts outstanding under the Loan will become due and payable. The Lender may at any time demand repayment of&#13;the Loan in whole or in part, in which case the Borrowers will be obligated to repay the Loan (or portion thereof for which repayment&#13;is demanded) within 30 days following the date of demand. The Borrowers may prepay the Loan, in whole or in part, at any time without&#13;penalty or premium.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Loan bears interest&#13;at a rate equal to the prime rate plus a spread of 2.49%, adjusted quarterly. Accrued interest is payable monthly, with the final&#13;installment of interest being due and payable on the Maturity Date. The Borrowers are also obligated to pay a servicing fee, unused&#13;commitment fee and origination fee in connection with the Loan. The Company paid $0.4 million in interest during the year ended&#13;December 31, 2020. The balance of the Loan was $6.4 million as of December 31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Loan Agreement contains&#13;affirmative and negative covenants that include covenants restricting each Company&amp;#8217;s ability to, among other things, incur&#13;indebtedness, grant liens, dispose of assets, merge or consolidate, make investments, or enter into restrictive agreements, subject&#13;to certain exceptions.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The obligations of the&#13;Borrowers under the Loan Agreement are secured by substantially all of their respective assets, except for accounts receivable&#13;and certain other specified excluded property.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Loan Agreement includes&#13;customary events of default that include among other things, non-payment defaults, covenant defaults, inaccuracy of representations&#13;and warranties, cross default to material indebtedness, bankruptcy and insolvency defaults and change in control defaults. Under&#13;certain circumstances, a default interest rate will apply on all obligations during the existence of an event of default under&#13;the Loan Agreement at a per annum rate equal to 2.00% above the applicable interest rate.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In connection with the&#13;Loan Agreement, the Company issued to the Lender a warrant to purchase up to 100,000 shares of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock&#13;at an initial exercise price of $3.94 per share (the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Warrant&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;). The Warrant expires on January 15, 2025. In&#13;connection with the issuance of the Warrant, the Company granted the Lender piggy-back registration rights with respect to the&#13;shares of common stock issuable upon exercise of the Warrant, subject to certain exceptions. On June 3, 2020, the Company entered&#13;into a Modification Agreement with Live Oak that made changes to the Financial Reports and Other Data Section and restated Exhibit&#13;B.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On January 16, 2020, in&#13;connection with the Company&amp;#8217;s consummation of the Loan Agreement, Eastside repaid in full and terminated the Secured Line&#13;of Credit Promissory Note that Eastside had issued to TQLA, LLC (&amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;Holder&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;) on November 29, 2019 (the &amp;#8220;&lt;u&gt;TQLA&#13;Note&lt;/u&gt;&amp;#8221;). Since Eastside repaid the TQLA Note in full prior to its maturity date, the Common Stock Purchase Warrant that&#13;Eastside had issued to Holder on November 29, 2019 is not be exercisable and is cancelled. No prepayment or early termination penalties&#13;were incurred by Eastside as a result of repaying the TQLA Note. In addition, Eastside repaid in full and terminated the $3.0 million&#13;credit and security agreement (the &amp;#8220;Credit and Security Agreement&amp;#8221;), by and between the Company and The KFK Children&amp;#8217;s&#13;Trust, Jeffrey Anderson &amp;#8211; Trustee (the &amp;#8220;Lender&amp;#8221;). The Company paid $0.1 million in interest on the TQLA Note&#13;and the Credit and Security Agreement during the first quarter of 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On May 13, 2020, Live Oak&#13;(the &amp;#8220;Lender&amp;#8221;) notified the Company that it was in technical default under certain covenants in a loan agreement, dated&#13;January 15, 2020, between the Company, Motherlode LLC, Big Bottom Distilling, LLC, Craft Canning + Bottling LLC, RRWC, Outlandish&#13;Beverages LLC, and Live Oak (the &amp;#8220;Loan Agreement&amp;#8221;). Those technical defaults included the failure to timely deliver&#13;information and its belief that the Company owed certain taxes and did not relate to any failure to pay amounts owing under the&#13;Loan Agreement. The Loan Agreement provides that upon an event of default, the Lender may, at its option, declare the entire loan&#13;to be immediately due and payable. Further, a default interest rate may apply on all obligations during the existence of an event&#13;of default at a per annum rate equal to 2.00% above the applicable interest rate. On June 3, 2020 the Company entered into a Second&#13;Modification to Loan Agreement (&amp;#8220;Modification&amp;#8221;) with the Lender agreeing to waive the technical defaults upon the satisfaction&#13;of certain conditions by September 30, 2020. The Company complied with these conditions and was compliant with the terms of&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On May 10, 2018, the Company&#13;entered into a credit and security agreement (the &amp;#8220;Credit and Security Agreement&amp;#8221;), by and between the Company and&#13;The KFK Children&amp;#8217;s Trust, Jeffrey Anderson &amp;#8211; Trustee (the &amp;#8220;Lender&amp;#8221;). Pursuant to the Credit and Security&#13;Agreement, the Lender will make loans to the Company in an aggregate principal amount not to exceed $3.0 million (the &amp;#8220;Loans&amp;#8221;).&#13;The Loans are secured by all of the Company&amp;#8217;s bulk whiskey, bourbon and rye inventory held in third-party storage facilities&#13;(&amp;#8220;Specified Inventory&amp;#8221;). The Company may borrow 80% of the value of the Specified Inventory it is able to purchase&#13;under the Credit and Security Agreement.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The proceeds of the Loans&#13;are to be used by the Company to purchase the Specified Inventory for use in distilling and producing its spirits products, and&#13;for no other purpose.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Loans have an annual&#13;interest rate of 7.00%. The Company will pay accrued and unpaid interest on the Loans, for the period commencing on the date each&#13;such Loan is made and continuing until each such Loan is paid in full. During 2019, The Company paid $0.2 million in interest on&#13;the Loans. The Company must pay the outstanding principal amount of the Loans in a one-time payment on the termination date of&#13;the Credit and Security Agreement (June 10, 2021), or earlier pursuant to other provisions thereof. The Company may prepay the&#13;Loans or any portion thereof at any time, and from time to time, without premium or penalty. As of December 31, 2019, the Company&#13;has borrowed the full $3.0 million available under the agreement. The Loans were paid in full on January 30, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The provision for income&#13;taxes results in effective tax rates which are different than the federal income tax statutory rate. The provision (benefit) for&#13;income taxes for the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019 were as follows, assuming a 21% federal effective tax rate. The Company&#13;also has a state tax rate for Oregon, of 6.6% for both December 31, 2020 and 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As of December 31, 2020,&#13;the Company has a cumulative net operating loss carryforward (NOL) of approximately $47.6 million, to offset against future income&#13;for federal and state tax purposes. These federal and state NOLs can be carried forward for 20 and 15 years, respectively. The&#13;federal NOLs begin to expire in 2034, and the state NOLs begin to expire in 2029. The utilization of the net operating loss carryforwards&#13;may be subject to substantial annual limitation due to ownership change provisions of the Internal Revenue Code of 1986 (as amended,&#13;the Internal Revenue Code) and similar state provisions. In general, if the Company experiences a greater than 50 percentage aggregate&#13;change in ownership of certain significant stockholders over a three-year period (a &amp;#8220;Section 382 ownership change&amp;#8221;),&#13;utilization of its pre-change NOL carryforwards are subject to an annual limitation under Section 382 of the Internal Revenue Code&#13;(and similar state laws). The annual limitation generally is determined by multiplying the value of the Company&amp;#8217;s stock at&#13;the time of such ownership change (subject to certain adjustments) by the applicable long-term tax-exempt rate. Such limitations&#13;may result in expiration of a portion of the NOL carryforwards before utilization and may be substantial.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;13. Commitments and Contingencies&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Legal Matters&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On December 15, 2020, Grover Wickersham&#13;filed a complaint in the United States District Court for the District Court of Oregon against the Company.&amp;#160; Mr. Wickersham, the&#13;former CEO and Chairman of the Board of the Company, has asserted causes of action for fraud in the inducement, breach of contract, breach&#13;of the implied covenant of good faith and fair dealing, defamation, interference with economic advantage, elder financial abuse, and dissemination&#13;of false and misleading proxy materials&amp;#160; The Company disputes the allegations and intends to defend the case vigorously.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;14. Net Loss per Common Share&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;15. Stockholder&amp;#8217;s Equity&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Issuance of Common Stock&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;During 2020, the Company&#13;issued 706,987 shares of common stock to directors, employees and consultants for stock-based compensation of $1.0 million. The&#13;shares were valued using the closing share price of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock on the date of grant, within the range of&#13;$1.08 to $3.20 per share.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;During 2019, the Company&#13;issued 291,099 shares of common stock to directors, employees and consultants for stock-based compensation of $1.7 million. The&#13;shares were valued using the closing share price of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock on the date of grant, within the range of&#13;$3.68 to $6.13 per share.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In September 2019, the&#13;Company issued 280,555 units (the &amp;#8220;Units&amp;#8221;) in connection with a private offering at a per Unit price of $4.50 per share,&#13;resulting in net proceeds of $1.3 million. Each Unit consists of one share of Eastside&amp;#8217;s common stock and a three-year warrant&#13;to acquire 0.5 shares of common stock at an exercise price of $5.50 per share.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In April 2019, the Company&#13;issued 1,077 shares of common stock in connection with existing option exercises at an exercise price of $3.99.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On January 11, 2019, the&#13;Company issued 338,212 shares of common stock in connection with the acquisition of Craft Canning for a total consideration of&#13;$2.1 million.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Stock-Based Compensation&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On September 8, 2016, the&#13;Company adopted the 2016 Equity Incentive Plan (the &amp;#8220;2016 Plan&amp;#8221;). Pursuant to the terms of the plan, on January 1,&#13;2020, the number of shares available for grant under the 2016 Plan reset to 2,887,005 shares, equal to 8% of the number of outstanding&#13;shares of the Company&amp;#8217;s capital stock, calculated on an as-converted basis, on December 31 of the preceding calendar year,&#13;and then added to the prior year plan amount. As of December 31, 2020, there were 134,514 options and 1,079,039 restricted stock&#13;units (&amp;#8220;RSUs&amp;#8221;) issued under the 2016 Plan, with vesting schedules varying between immediate or three (3) years from&#13;the grant date.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On January 29, 2015, our&#13;Board of Directors adopted the 2015 Stock Incentive Plan (the &amp;#8220;2015 Plan&amp;#8221;). The total number of shares available for&#13;the grant of either stock options or compensation stock under the plan is 50,000 shares, subject to adjustment. As of December&#13;31, 2020, no options under the Plan remain outstanding.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company also issues,&#13;from time to time, options that are not registered under a formal option plan. As of December 31, 2020, there were no options outstanding&#13;that were not issued under the Plans.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

   &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;$&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom: black 2.25pt double; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;4.04&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=padding-bottom: 2.5pt&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The aggregate intrinsic&#13;value of options outstanding as of December 31, 2020 was $0 million.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As of December 31, 2020,&#13;there were 46,292 unvested options with an aggregate grant date fair value of $0.1 million. The unvested options will vest in accordance&#13;with the vesting schedule in each respective option agreement, which varies between immediate and five (5) years from the grant&#13;date. The aggregate intrinsic value of unvested options as of December 31, 2020 was $0 million. During the year ended December&#13;31, 2020, 39,222 options vested.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company uses the Black-Scholes&#13;valuation model to measure the grant-date fair value of stock options. The grant-date fair value of stock options issued to employees&#13;is recognized on a straight-line basis over the requisite service period. Stock-based awards issued to nonemployees are recorded&#13;at fair value on the measurement date and are subject to periodic market adjustments as the underlying stock-based awards vest.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;To determine the fair value&#13;of stock options using the Black-Scholes valuation model, the calculation takes into consideration the effect of the following:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 48px&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 24px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Exercise price of the option&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the Company&amp;#8217;s common stock on the date of grant&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Expected term of the option&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Expected volatility over the expected term of the option&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&amp;#9679;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Risk-free interest rate for the expected term of the option&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The calculation includes&#13;several assumptions that require management&amp;#8217;s judgment. The expected term of the options is calculated using the simplified&#13;method described in GAAP. The simplified method defines the expected term as the average of the contractual term and the vesting&#13;period. Estimated volatility is derived from volatility calculated using historical closing prices of common shares of similar&#13;entities whose share prices are publicly available for the expected term of the options. The risk-free interest rate is based on&#13;the U.S. Treasury constant maturities in effect at the time of grant for the expected term of the options.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company did not issue&#13;any additional options during the year ended December 31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The following is a description&#13;of transactions since January 1, 2019 as to which the amount involved exceeds the lesser of $0.1 million or one percent (1%) of&#13;the average of total assets at year-end for the last two completed fiscal years which was $0.3 million and in which any related&#13;person has or will have a direct or indirect material interest, other than equity, compensation, termination and other arrangements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On June 11, 2019, the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;Board appointed Owen Lingley to the Board to fill an existing vacancy on the Board effective immediately. Owen Lingley is the founder&#13;of Craft Canning, LLC, which was acquired by the Company on January 11, 2019 and subsequently changed its name to Craft Canning&#13;+ Bottling LLC. In connection with the acquisition of Craft Canning, Mr. Lingley received $1.8 million in cash, 338,212 shares&#13;of common stock of the Company and a promissory note in the aggregate principal amount of $0.7 million which bears interest at&#13;a rate of 5% per annum and matures on January 11, 2022. The shares acquired by Mr. Lingley in connection with the acquisition of&#13;Craft Canning are subject to a one-year lock-up restriction and have &amp;#8220;piggyback&amp;#8221; registration rights effective after&#13;the one-year lock-up. Mr. Lingley resigned from the Board on November 18, 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In addition, the Company&#13;also issued to Mr. Lingley a warrant to purchase 146,262 shares of common stock of the Company at $7.80 per share and an exercise&#13;period of three years. The shares of common stock issuable upon exercise of the warrant will be subject to the same &amp;#8220;piggyback&amp;#8221;&#13;registration rights as the shares received in connection with the acquisition of Craft Canning, described above.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Following the acquisition&#13;of Craft Canning, Mr. Lingley became non-executive Chairman of Craft Canning and is party to a consulting agreement with the Company.&#13;Under his consulting agreement with the Company, Mr. Lingley receives annual cash compensation of $0.1 million per year. Mr. Lingley&#13;resigned as non-executive Chairman of Craft Canning in January 2020, and under the terms of his consulting agreement 146,262 warrants&#13;were cancelled.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On October 24, 2019, the&#13;Company&amp;#8217;s Board appointed Stephanie Kilkenny to the Board to fill an existing vacancy on the Board effective immediately.&#13;Stephanie Kilkenny was the former managing director of Azu&amp;#241;ia Tequila, and together with her spouse, owns and controls TQLA,&#13;LLC (&amp;#8220;TQLA&amp;#8221;), the majority owner of Intersect. In connection with the acquisition of Azu&amp;#241;ia Tequila from Intersect,&#13;TQLA is entitled to receive up to 93.88% of the aggregate consideration payable under the asset purchase agreement. Subject to&#13;compliance with applicable Nasdaq rules, aggregate initial consideration will be payable approximately 18 months following the&#13;closing and will consist of 850,000 shares of Company common stock at a stipulated value of $6.00 per share, 350,000 shares of&#13;Company common stock based on the Company&amp;#8217;s stock price twelve months after the close of the transaction, and additional&#13;shares based on the Azu&amp;#241;ia business achieving certain revenue targets and the Company&amp;#8217;s stock price 18 months after&#13;the close of the transaction. The Company has also agreed to issue additional stock consideration (subject to compliance with applicable&#13;Nasdaq rules) of up to $1.5 million upon the Azu&amp;#241;ia business achieving revenue of at least $9.45 million in the period commencing&#13;on the 13th month following the closing and ending on the 24th month following the closing.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;In addition, on September&#13;16, 2019, the Company entered into a Subscription Agreement with Stephanie Kilkenny&amp;#8217;s spouse, Patrick J. Kilkenny as Trustee&#13;For Patrick J. Kilkenny Revocable Trust (the &amp;#8220;Kilkenny Trust&amp;#8221;), in reliance on the exemption from registration afforded&#13;by Section 4(a)(2) of the Securities Act and Rule 506(b) promulgated thereunder, pursuant to which the Company agreed to issue&#13;and sell to the Kilkenny Trust an aggregate of 55,555 units at a per unit price of $4.50. Each unit consists of one share of the&#13;Company&amp;#8217;s common stock and a three-year warrant to acquire 0.5 shares of common stock at an exercise price of $5.50 per share.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

The Note matures&#13;on April 15, 2020 and may be prepaid in whole or in part at any time without penalty or premium. Repayment of the Note is subject&#13;to acceleration in the event of an event of default. The Company may use the proceeds to purchase tequila for its Azu&amp;#241;ia product&#13;line and for general corporate purposes, as approved by the Holder. As of December 31, 2019, the Company has borrowed $1.0 million&#13;on the Note. Stephanie Kilkenny, a director of the Company, owns and controls TQLA with her spouse. The Company&amp;#8217;s Audit Committee&#13;approved the transaction. The Note was paid in full in January 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.25in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.25in&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;On February 5, 2021, the Company repaid other liabilities due to Intersect&#13;and TQLA in an amount of $0.7 million. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;&lt;u&gt;Other&lt;/u&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 6pt&gt;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;&lt;td style=width: 0.25in&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=width: 0.25in&gt;&lt;font style=font: 10pt Symbol&gt;&amp;#183;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;On January 22, 2021, the Company was notified by the Alcohol and Tobacco&#13;Tax and Trade Bureau (TTB) that it will conduct a tax review of Motherlode, LLC, Eastside Distilling, Inc and Big Bottom Distilling, LLC&#13;for the period January 2019 to present. The purpose of the examination is to determine whether the distilled spirits plant is in compliance&#13;with certain applicable federal laws and regulations relating to the production and payment of excise tax of distilled spirits, and review&#13;internal controls and systems, and records examination. In connection with the examination, the Company recorded $0.1 million of additional&#13;excise taxes as of December 31, 2020. &lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellpadding=0 cellspacing=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman

The shares were valued using the closing share price of the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;common stock on the date of the grant of $1.50 per share.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Revenue Recognition&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Net sales include product&#13;sales, less excise taxes and customer programs and incentives. The Company recognizes revenue by applying the following steps in&#13;accordance with Accounting Standards Codification (&amp;#8220;ASC&amp;#8221;) Topic 606 &amp;#8211; &lt;i&gt;Revenue from Contracts with Customers&lt;/i&gt;:&#13;(1) identify the contract with a customer; (2) identify the performance obligations in the contract; (3) determine the transaction&#13;price; (4) allocate the transaction price to each performance obligation in the contract; and (5) recognize revenue when each performance&#13;obligation is satisfied.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Discontinued Operations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The Company reports discontinued&#13;operations by applying the following criteria in accordance with ASC Topic 205-20 &amp;#8211; &lt;i&gt;Presentation of Financial Statements&#13;&amp;#8211; Discontinued Operations&lt;/i&gt;: (1) Component of an entity; (2) Held for sale criteria; and (3) Strategic shift.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On December 31, 2019, management&#13;made a strategic shift to focus the Company&amp;#8217;s sales and marketing efforts on the nationally branded product platform, resulting&#13;in the decision to close all four of its retail stores in the Portland, Oregon area. Although this decision meets the criteria&#13;(1) and (3) for reporting discontinued operations, it did not meet the (2) Held for sale criteria until the retail stores were&#13;closed or abandoned, which occurred by March 31, 2020.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;On October 29, 2020, the&#13;Company announced its intent to divest its Redneck Riviera Spirits business. The Company signed a non-binding term sheet between&#13;Eastside and Rich Marks, LLC, Redneck Riviera Whiskey Co, LLC (&amp;#8220;RRWC&amp;#8221;), John D. Rich Tisa Trust and Redneck Spirits&#13;Group, LLC (collectively the buyers referred to as &amp;#8220;RSG&amp;#8221;) whereby RSG would pay a termination fee as well as purchase&#13;certain assets from the Company which could include raw materials and finished goods. The total consideration was estimated to&#13;be $8.1 million inclusive of a $3 million dollar termination fee and the remainder of proceeds from selling RSG raw materials and&#13;finished goods. The divesture is subject to negotiation and execution of definitive agreements. On February 8, 2021, the Company&#13;completed the sale of its Redneck Riviera Spirits business.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As of and for the year&#13;ended December 31, 2020, the assets, liabilities, revenue, expenses and cash flows from retail operations and the RRWC business&#13;have been classified as discontinued operations separately from continuing operations. For comparative purposes, prior period amounts&#13;have been reclassified to conform to current period presentation.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Cash and Cash Equivalents&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Concentrations&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Fair Value Measurements&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;GAAP defines fair value,&#13;establishes a framework for measuring fair value, and requires certain disclosures about fair value measurements. GAAP permits&#13;an entity to choose to measure many financial instruments and certain other items at fair value and contains financial statement&#13;presentation and disclosure requirements for assets and liabilities for which the fair value option is elected. As of December&#13;31, 2020 and 2019, management has not elected to report any of the Company&amp;#8217;s assets or liabilities at fair value under the&#13;&amp;#8220;fair value option&amp;#8221; provided by GAAP.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The hierarchy of fair value&#13;valuation techniques under GAAP provides for three levels: Level 1 provides the most reliable measure of fair value, whereas Level&#13;3, if applicable, generally would require significant management judgment. The three levels for categorizing assets and liabilities&#13;under GAAP&amp;#8217;s fair value measurement requirements are as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; border-collapse: collapse&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 62px&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 62px&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 1:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using cash or unadjusted quoted prices in active markets for identical assets or liabilities.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: top&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 2:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using inputs other than quoted prices that are observable for the applicable asset or liability, either directly or indirectly, such as quoted prices for similar (as opposed to identical) assets or liabilities in active markets and quoted prices for identical or similar assets or liabilities in markets that are not active.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Level 3:&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Fair value of the asset or liability is determined using unobservable inputs that are significant to the fair value measurement and reflect management&amp;#8217;s own assumptions regarding the applicable asset or liability.&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;None of the Company&amp;#8217;s&#13;assets or liabilities were measured at fair value as of December 31, 2020 or 2019. However, GAAP requires the disclosure of fair&#13;value information about financial instruments that are not measured at fair value. Financial instruments consist principally of&#13;trade receivables, accounts payable, accrued liabilities, notes payable, convertible note payable and the secured credit facility.&#13;The estimated fair value of trade receivables, accounts payable, and accrued liabilities approximates their carrying value due&#13;to the short period of time to their maturities. As of December 31, 2020 and 2019, the Company&amp;#8217;s notes are payable at fixed&#13;rates and their carrying value approximates fair value.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Items Measured at Fair Value on a Nonrecurring&#13;Basis&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;Income Taxes&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;The provision for income&#13;taxes is based on income and expenses as reported for financial statement purposes using the &amp;#8220;asset and liability method&amp;#8221;&#13;for accounting for deferred taxes. Deferred tax assets and liabilities are recognized for the future tax consequences attributable&#13;to differences between the financial statement carrying amounts of existing assets and liabilities and their respective tax bases.&#13;Deferred tax assets and liabilities are reflected at currently enacted income tax rates applicable to the period in which the deferred&#13;tax assets or liabilities are expected to be realized or settled.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;As changes in tax laws&#13;or rates are enacted, deferred tax assets and liabilities are adjusted through the provision for income taxes. A valuation allowance,&#13;if needed, reduces deferred tax assets to the amount expected to be realized. As of December 31, 2020 and 2019, the Company established&#13;valuation allowances against its net deferred tax assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27.35pt; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Income tax positions that&#13;meet the &amp;#8220;more-likely-than-not&amp;#8221; recognition threshold are measured at the largest amount of income tax benefit that&#13;is more than 50% likely to be realized upon settlement with the applicable taxing authority. The portion of the benefits associated&#13;with income tax positions taken that exceeds the amount measured as described above would be reflected as a liability for unrecognized&#13;income tax benefits in the accompanying consolidated balance sheets along with any associated interest and penalties that would&#13;be payable to the taxing authorities upon examination. Interest and penalties associated with unrecognized income tax benefits&#13;would be classified as additional income taxes in the accompanying consolidated statements of operations. There were no unrecognized&#13;income tax benefits, nor any interest and penalties associated with unrecognized income tax benefits, accrued or expensed at and&#13;for the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0 0 0 27pt; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman

 Serif; margin: 0&gt;&lt;b&gt;1. Description of Business&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; word-spacing: 0px; text-align: center&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; word-spacing: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Eastside Distilling&#13;(the &amp;#8220;Company&amp;#8221; or &amp;#8220;Eastside Distilling) was incorporated under the laws of Nevada in 2004 under the name of Eurocan&#13;Holdings, Ltd. In December 2014, the Company changed its corporate name to Eastside Distilling, Inc. to reflect the acquisition of Eastside&#13;Distilling, LLC. The Company manufactures, acquires, blends, bottles, imports, exports, markets and sells a wide variety of alcoholic&#13;beverages under recognized brands. The Company currently employ&amp;#160;78&amp;#160;people in the United States.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; word-spacing: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;b&gt;2. Liquidity&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; word-spacing: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; word-spacing: 0px; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;Historically,&#13;the Company has funded its cash and liquidity needs through operating cash flow, convertible notes, extended credit terms, and equity&#13;financings. For the years ended December 31, 2020 and 2019, the Company incurred a net loss of approximately $9.9 million and $16.9 million,&#13;respectively, and has an accumulated deficit of approximately $54.1 million as of December 31, 2020. The Company has been dependent on&#13;raising capital from debt and equity financings to meet its needs for cash flow used in operating activities. For the year ended December&#13;31, 2020, the Company raised approximately $3.4 million in additional capital through equity and debt financing (net of repayments).&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
